cambiumHWInfo  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (-1..6|8..14|16..20|22|33..55|59..62|100..250)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Hardware SKU:
			-1 - Not available

		DESCRIPTION

			And Uplink MCS Rate for 802.11ax standard devices.

			802.11n HW:

			1  for MCS1,
			2  for MCS2,
			3  for MCS3,
			4  for MCS4,
			5  for MCS5,

			20 for 'SS MCS 0 - BPSK 1/2',
			21 for 'SS MCS 1 - QPSK 1/2',
			22 for 'SS MCS 2 - QPSK 3/4',
			23 for 'SS MCS 3 - 16-QAM 1/2',
			24 for 'SS MCS 4 - 16-QAM 3/4',
			25 for 'SS MCS 5 - 64-QAM 2/3',
			26 for 'SS MCS 6 - 64-QAM 3/4',
			27 for 'SS MCS 7 - 64-QAM 5/6',
			28 for 'SS MCS 8 - 256-QAM 3/4',
			29 for 'SS MCS 9 - 256-QAM 5/6',

			30 for 'DS MCS 0 - BPSK 1/2',
			31 for 'DS MCS 1 - QPSK 1/2',
			32 for 'DS MCS 2 - QPSK 3/4',
			33 for 'DS MCS 3 - 16-QAM 1/2',
			34 for 'DS MCS 4 - 16-QAM 3/4',
			35 for 'DS MCS 5 - 64-QAM 2/3',
			36 for 'DS MCS 6 - 64-QAM 3/4',
			37 for 'DS MCS 7 - 64-QAM 5/6',
			38 for 'DS MCS 8 - 256-QAM 3/4',
			39 for 'DS MCS 9 - 256-QAM 5/6',

			802.11ax HW:

			MCS rate on AX is in range of 100-811 and organized using the following format:
			NSS * 100 + MCS.
			Where NSS is a Number of Spatial Streams: 1-8
			      MCS is Modulation and Coding Scheme: 0-11
			0  for 'MCS 0  - BPSK 1/2',
			1  for 'MCS 1  - QPSK 1/2',
			2  for 'MCS 2  - QPSK 3/4',
			3  for 'MCS 3  - 16-QAM 1/2',
			4  for 'MCS 4  - 16-QAM 3/4',
			5  for 'MCS 5  - 64-QAM 2/3',
			6  for 'MCS 6  - 64-QAM 3/4',
			7  for 'MCS 7  - 64-QAM 5/6',
			8  for 'MCS 8  - 256-QAM 3/4',
			9  for 'MCS 9  - 256-QAM 5/6',
			10 for 'MCS 10 - 1024-QAM 3/6',
			11 for 'MCS 11 - 1024-QAM 5/6',

		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { cambiumRFStatus 6 }

			11 for 'MCS 11 - 1024-QAM 5/6',

		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { cambiumRFStatus 7 }

	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (1..15|20..29|30..39)

			1 for MCS1,

			11 for MCS11,
			12 for MCS12,
			13 for MCS13,
			14 for MCS14,
			15 for MCS15,

			(Values in brackets represent IEEE 802.11ac rate codes)

			20 (0x80) for 'SS MCS 0 - BPSK 1/2',
			21 (0x81) for 'SS MCS 1 - QPSK 1/2',
			22 (0x82) for 'SS MCS 2 - QPSK 3/4',
			23 (0x83) for 'SS MCS 3 - 16-QAM 1/2',
			24 (0x84) for 'SS MCS 4 - 16-QAM 3/4',
			25 (0x85) for 'SS MCS 5 - 64-QAM 2/3',
			26 (0x86) for 'SS MCS 6 - 64-QAM 3/4',
			27 (0x87) for 'SS MCS 7 - 64-QAM 5/6',
			28 (0x88) for 'SS MCS 8 - 256-QAM 3/4',
			29 (0x89) for 'SS MCS 9 - 256-QAM 5/6',

			30 (0xd0) for 'DS MCS 0 - BPSK 1/2',
			31 (0xd1) for 'DS MCS 1 - QPSK 1/2',
			32 (0xd2) for 'DS MCS 2 - QPSK 3/4',
			33 (0xd3) for 'DS MCS 3 - 16-QAM 1/2',
			34 (0xd4) for 'DS MCS 4 - 16-QAM 3/4',
			35 (0xd5) for 'DS MCS 5 - 64-QAM 2/3',
			36 (0xd6) for 'DS MCS 6 - 64-QAM 3/4',
			37 (0xd7) for 'DS MCS 7 - 64-QAM 5/6',
			38 (0xd8) for 'DS MCS 8 - 256-QAM 3/4',
			39 (0xd9) for 'DS MCS 9 - 256-QAM 5/6'

		Device Allocation: AP"
	::= { cambiumAPConnectedSTAListEntry 8 }

cambiumSTADropReason OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   DisplayString (SIZE(0..64))
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
			"AP Reject reasons:
				1 - Max capacity reached
				2 - Software versions incompatible
				3 - PTP mode (ACL policy)
				4 - STA in blacklist
				5 - Other reason
				6 - STA ranging failed
				7 - Malformed INAR
				8 - ePMP Elevate license exceeded
			 STA Association failure reasons:
				16 - INA retries exhausted
				17 - Out of cell
				18 - Error prop delay calculation
				19 - Lost AID
				20 - Authentication failed
				21 - Certificate check failed
				22 - Generic auth fail
				23 - MAC versions incompatible
				24 - INA response not received
				25 - Frame duration not supported
				30 - AP doesn't support reject reason
			 STA Disassociation reasons:
				32 - No allocation on AP
				33 - GPFs miss
				34 - BEACONs miss
				35 - STA has detected radar (ETSI)
				36 - STA initiated disconnect
				37 - AP parameters changed
				38 - Elevate auth failed due to packet loss
				39 - AP initiated disconnect by peer radio
				40 - STA KeepAlive RX stuck
			 AP Disassociation reasons:
				48 - Communication loss
				49 - Invalid key
				50 - Operator initiated disconnect
				51 - AP initiated disconnect
				52 - INAC miss timeout
				53 - AP KeepAlive RX stuck"
	::= { cambiumRFStatus 61 }

cambiumGPSFirmwareUpdateStatus	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..10)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Software Update Status OID
			0 - No GPS FW Update is progress or No FW update is required,
			1 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Uploading SW package to device,
			2 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Verifying SHA2 signature,
			3 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Executing pre-update script,
			4 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Uploading Firmware to GPS device,
			5 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Uploading Firmware to GPS device,
			6 - GPS FW Update is in progress, Executing post-update script,
			7 - GPS FW Update is finished, waiting for reboot,
			8 - GPS FW Update is Required, Please upgrade to latest GPS FW,
		When GPS FW Update is successfully, return value is 7,
		GUI or NMS indicate that GPS FW update was successful,
		Device can be rebooted.
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	::= { cambiumGPSStatus 10}

TddSyncStatEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	tddSyncStatPeriod
		INTEGER,
	tddSyncPulseCount
	    Counter32,
	tddSyncLostPulseCount
		Counter32,
	tddSyncInvalidPulseCount
		Counter32,
	tddSyncInvPulseDeviationMin
		Integer32,
	tddSyncInvPulseDeviationMax
		Integer32,
	tddSyncInvPulseDeviationAvgAbs
		Integer32,
	tddSyncDriftMin
		Integer32,
	tddSyncDriftMax
		Integer32,
	tddSyncDriftAvg
		Integer32,
	tddSyncJitterMin
		Integer32,
	tddSyncJitterMax
		Integer32,
	tddSyncJitterAvgAbs
		Integer32,
	tddSyncState1Count
		Counter32,
	tddSyncState1Duration
		Counter32,
	tddSyncState2Count
		Counter32,
	tddSyncState2Duration
		Counter32,
	tddSyncState3Count
		Counter32,
	tddSyncState3Duration
		Counter32
}

tddSyncStatPeriod OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX    INTEGER {
				minutes5(1), -- statistics for last 5 minutes
				hours1(2),   -- statistics for last hour  (+- 5 minutes)
				hours24(3),  -- statistics for last 24 hours (+- 1hour)
				alltime(4)   -- statistics for all the time
			  }
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The Time period the Sync statistics is taken for
		Device Allocation: AP"
	::= {tddSyncStatEntry 1}

lanSwitchPortPerfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     LanSwitchPortPerfEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Switch performance monitoring
                Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	INDEX	{ lanSwitchPortsNum }
	::= { lanSwitchPortPerfTable 1 }

LanSwitchPortPerfEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	rxSwitchPortKBCount
		Counter64,
	rxSwitchPortTotalPacketCount
		Counter64,
	rxSwitchPortErrorPacketCount
		Counter64,
	rxSwitchPortUnicastPacketCount
		Counter64,
	rxSwitchPortMulticastPacketCount
		Counter64,
	rxSwitchPortBroadcastPacketCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortKBCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortTotalPacketCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortErrorPacketCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortUnicastPacketCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortMulticastPacketCount
		Counter64,
	txSwitchPortBroadcastPacketCount
		Counter64
}

dhcpLanHostTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF DhcpLanHostEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Table for DHCP Hosts
		Device Allocation: SM"
	::= { cambiumDHCP 5 }

dhcpLanHostEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	DhcpLanHostEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"DHCP Hosts Table Entry
		Device Allocation: SM"
	INDEX	{ dhcpLanHostIndex }
	::= { dhcpLanHostTable 1 }

DhcpLanHostEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	dhcpLanHostIndex
		Integer32,
	dhcpLanHostIP
		IpAddress,
	dhcpLanHostMAC
		DisplayString,
	dhcpLanHostName
		DisplayString
}

		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..8)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"DHCP host Table Index
		Table Entry is cleared if Index is set to zero
		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { dhcpLanHostEntry 1 }

		 0 - Connecting to License Server,
		 1 - Connected. ePMP Elevate Subscriber Module Limit synced with License Server,
		 2 - Connected. ePMP Elevate Subscriber Module Limit Exceeded,
		 2004 - Units are not supported with limited concurrency,
		 2012 - Not authorized to process any request,
		 2015 - Internal error,
		 2018 - License is expired,
		 2019 - License is disabled,
		 2023 - License does not exist or license is not in active state,
		 2024 - Invalid parameter,
		 2025 - Session terminated,
		 2026 - Access denied to the requested feature,
		 2031 - No authorization server mapped to given vendorId
		 Device Allocation: AP"

        SYNTAX     Integer32 (0|1)
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS     obsolete
        DESCRIPTION
		"GPS Lock.
		This field indicates if the GPS Key is OK. Based on this the GPS
		is locked on the board.
			0 - GPS Key is bad. Sync Source defaulted to Internal GPS only
			1 - GPS Key is good. User can set sync source to any value
		Device Allocation: AP"
        DEFVAL  { 0 }
        ::= { systemConfig 10 }

systemConfigGPSLockBit  OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX     Integer32 (0..2)
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS     obsolete
        DESCRIPTION
                "GPS Lock Bit.
                This bit indicates if the GPS feature Lock Bit is set or not.
                If the hardware bit is set then GPS synchronisation can't be used.
                        0 - No limitation of usage GPS synchronisation,
                        1 - GPS synchronisation not allowed,

		prefferedListTableEntryIndex
				Integer32,
		prefferedListTableEntrySSID
				OCTET STRING,
		prefferedListTableEntryKEY
				OCTET STRING,
		prefferedListTableSecurityMethod
				Integer32
}

prefferedListTableEntryIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..16)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"Preferred AP Table Index
		Table Entry is cleared if Index is set to zero
		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { prefferedAPEntry 1 }

prefferedListTableEntrySSID	 OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   OCTET STRING (SIZE(0|1..32))
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"Preferred AP SSID
		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { prefferedAPEntry 2 }

prefferedListTableEntryKEY	OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   OCTET STRING (SIZE(0|8..63))
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"Preferred AP Shared Key
		Device Allocation: SM"
		::= { prefferedAPEntry 3 }

prefferedListTableSecurityMethod  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32(0..6)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"Authentication modes to connect to AP
		Device Allocation: SM
		Use bitmask to enable pereferred methods, 0 - means enable method:
		set 0-th bit to 0 - Open method (110b)
		set 1-st bit to 0 - WPA2 method (101b)
		set 2-nd bit to 0 - EAP-TTLS method (011b)
		0x00 - All enabled"
		DEFVAL	{ 0 }
		::= { prefferedAPEntry 4 }


cambiumpmp80211DeviceReboot	 OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (1)
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"OID for Device Reboot, send reboot command to device
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 1 }

cambiumpmp80211ConfigurationReset  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..7)
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"OID for System Configuration reset to Defaults
		Device Allocation: AP, SM
		Use bitmask to enable options:
		set 0-th bit to 1 to do reset at all (001b)
		set 1-st bit to 1 to preserve license (011b)
		set 2-nd bit to 1 to preserve passwords (101b)"
	::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 2 }

cambiumpmp80211ConfigurationSave  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (1)
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"OID for configuration save
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 3 }

		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (1)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"OID for configuration Discard
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
		::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 5 }

cambiumpmp80211ConfigurationState  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..255)
		MAX-ACCESS read-only
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
		"System configuration state OID.
		Bit masks:
			0000 0001 - System is configured.
			0000 0010 - There are unsaved changesets.
			0000 0100 - There are unrestarted services.
			0000 1000 - Needed reboot of the system.
			0001 0000 - Configurations was reset.
			0010 0000 - Services restarting in process.
			0100 0000 - Software Update performed.
			1000 0000 - IP Address or protocol was changed.
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
		::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 6 }

cambiumpmp80211SoftwareUpdate  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   OCTET STRING
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"System OID for Software Update Agent,
		SW Update link value can be either remote firmware link (http, https, ftp),
		or local file link: /tmp/firmware.tar.gz
		NOTE: Device is automatically rebooted if link type is remote
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 7 }

cambiumpmp80211SoftwareUpdateStatus	 OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..10)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS	   current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Software Update Status OID
			0 - No SW Update is pending or No SW upgrade occurs,
			1 - SW Update is in progress, Uploading image to device,
			2 - SW Update is in progress, Verifying SHA2 signature,
			3 - SW Update is in progress, Executing pre-update script,
			4 - SW Update is in progress, Uploading image to flash,
			5 - SW Update is in progress, Uploading u-boot to flash,
			6 - SW Update is in progress, Executing post-update script,
			7 - SW Update is finished, waiting for reboot,
			8 - SW Update is in progress, Executing config down-grade script,
			9 - SW Update is in progress, Uploading firmware to flash & Reboot,
			10 - SW Update is in progress, Rebooting...
		When SW Update is successfully, return value is 7 for ePMP 1000/2000,
		and 9 for ePMP Elevate
		GUI or NMS indicate that SW update was successful,
		Device can be rebooted.
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 8 }

cambiumpmp80211SoftwareUpdateError  OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX     Integer32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS     current
        DESCRIPTION
	  "Software Update error code:
		0 - Finished successfully, waiting for reboot.
		1 - SW update file download failed.
		2 - Unpack failed, damaged or wrong format package.
		3 - Firmware digital signature check failed.
		4 - U-Boot digital signature check failed.
		5 - Firmware FLASH write failed.
		6 - U-Boot FLASH write failed.
		7 - Boot partition switch failed.
		8 - Board SKU is not supported for this firmware.
		9 - Can't read firmware version, upgrade is impossible.
		10 - Down-grade not supported for WiFi & ePTP modes.
		11 - Down-grade below 2.3.1 is not supported for AP Lite device.
		12 - Down-grade not supported for non SM TDD mode.
		13 - Down-grade below 2.4.2 not supported for Force180/200 board types.
		14 - Down-grade below 2.5.0 not supported for AP WiFi.
		15 - Down-grade below 2.4.3 not supported for Reset Via Power Sequence.
		16 - Down-grade below 2.4.3 not supported for Particular Country Locked device.
		17 - Down-grade below 2.5.0 not supported for 2.5ms mode.
		18 - Down-grade below 2.5.2 not supported for Use MAC Address as EAP-TTLS Username.
		19 - Down-grade below 2.6.0 not supported for 5/10Mhz BW for WiFi & ePTP mode.
		20 - Separate Management IP Port Forwarding and Data Port Mapping are not supported in SW versions below 2.6.0.
		21 - General error. Device has no free memory.
		22 - General error code.
		23 - Downgrade below release 3.0 is not supported for ePMP2000.
		24 - Incorrect firmware type for the current device type.
		25 - Firmware file format is wrong for the current device type.
		26 - Downgrade below 5.6.6 is not supported for ePMP-Elevate board type.
		27 - Downgrade below 3.0.1 is not supported for 2.5G board type.
		28 - Downgrade below 3.1 is not supported if Preffered AP Table contains SSIDs with spaces.
		29 - Manifest Digital signature check failed.
		30 - Downgrade below 3.4 is not supported for Force 190 boards.
		31 - Downgrade below 3.5.2 is not supported for 6 GHz board type.
		32 - Downgrade below 3.4 is not supported for Elevate 2.4 GHz board.
		33 - Versions below 3.5 do not support License Server. Disable the License Server option before downgrade.
		34 - Opening binary sw-upgrader failed.
		35 - General error of upgrade process.
		36 - Channel Bonding is not supported in SW versions below 4.1.1.
		37 - 80 MHz channel bandwidth is not supported in SW versions below 4.1.1.
		38 - NAT and Router modes are not supported in SW versions below 4.3.
		39 - Downgrade below 3.5.4 is not supported for 802.11n devices and below 4.3 for 802.11ac devices with MAC addresses from pool 58:C1:7A:xx:xx:xx.
		40 - MTU value other than 1538 is not supported in SW versions below 4.1.3.
		41 - Downgrade below 4.3 is not supported for Force 300-16 boards.
		42 - Membership VLAN/VLAN Mapping is not supported in SW versions below 4.3.
		43 - Downgrade below 4.3 is not supported for ePMP3000 boards.
		44 - 40 or 80 MHz channel bandwidth is not supported for ePMP3000 in SW versions below 4.3.1.
		45 - Cannot upgrade this device with IPv6 enabled.
		46 - Software Upgrade is Rejected because Trial Configuration is in progress.
		47 - Downgrade below 4.4 is not supported for Force 300-13 or Force 300-19 boards.
		48 - Downgrade below 4.5 is not supported for ePMP MP 3000 board.
		49 - ePTP mode is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		50 - 2.5 ms mode is not supported in SW versions below 4.6.
		51 - 5/10Mhz BW mode is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		52 - Reliable multicast is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		53 - ACS is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		54 - Standard WiFi Driver Mode is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		55 - Omni/Split-Sector Antenna is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		56 - Downgrade below 4.5.4 is not supported for 802.11n devices with MAC addresses from pool BC:E6:7C:xx:xx:xx.
		57 - ACS/DCS is not supported in SW versions below 4.5.
		58 - MTU value above 1700 is not supported in SW versions below 4.6.
		59 - Downgrade below 4.6 is not supported for MIPS based boards.
		60 - 70/30 65/35 60/40 55/45 45/55 40/60 35/65 downlink/uplink ratios are not supported in SW versions below 4.6.
		61 - cnVision devices aren't supported in SW versions below 4.6.
		62 - Downgrade below 4.6.1 is not supported for Force 300-25 V2 board.
		63 - Downgrade below 4.7 is not supported for Force 200L.
		64 - Cannot downgrade below 4.6.1 if DL Max Rate is not set to Use AP's config.
		65 - DPI is not supported in SW versions below 4.7.
		66 - WLR Driver Mode is not supported in SW versions below 5.2.0.
		67 - Downgrade below 5.2 is not supported for 6GHz boards.
		68 - Intelbras or Mikrotik licenses activated. Versions below 4.7 don't support those.
		69 - Downgrade below 4.7 is not supported for boards with soft country lock set.
		70 - Downgrade below 5.3 is not supported for the current hardware type.
		71 - Downgrade below 4.7 is not supported for boards with flexible mode selected.
		72 - Downgrade below 4.7 is not supported for boards with Port Forwarding configured containing ports 22(SSH), 161(SNMP), 80(HTTP), 443(HTTPS)
		73 - TR-069 option is not supported in SW versions below 5.2 on 802.11ax devices and 4.7 on other devices.
		74 - Downgrade below 4.6.4 is not supported for this device hardware.
				Device Allocation: AP, SM"
		::= { cambiumpmp80211SystemActions 13 }

cambiumpmp80211GPSSyncStatusTrap NOTIFICATION-TYPE
		OBJECTS { cambiumToolbarGPSSyncStateStr }

dpiLogLevel OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE(0..16))
	MAX-ACCESS  read-write
	STATUS      current
	DESCRIPTION
		"DPI log levels:
			off - disable logging;
			error - log when error occurs;
			warn - log to make a warning;
			notice - normal but significant condition;
			info - normal information message;
			debug - printed in debug mode;
			trace - detailed messages;
			func - function call trace;
			all - Enable all log levels;
			system - use the highest level from syslogServerLogMask.
		In case non of these values is set, the logging level from
		syslogServerLogMask is going to be used.
		All log messages are printed to the kernel log.
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	DEFVAL  { "system" }
	::= { dpi 3 }

	SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE(0..256))
	MAX-ACCESS  read-write
	STATUS      current
	DESCRIPTION
		"DPI log components:
			sys - system;
			mem - memory;
			pkt - packet;
			flow - flow;
			tcp - tcp;
			udp - udp;
			session - tcp session;
			tcp_pkt - trace tcp packet;
			udp_pkt - trace udp packet;
			icmp_pkt - trace icmp packet;
			other_pkt - trace other packet;
			mac - trace mac info;
			http - http;
			https - https;
			quic - quic;
			ftp - ftp;
			mail - mail;
			urinorm - http filter urinorm;
			apg - application guard;
			av - antivirus;
			dna - antivirus engine;
			decomp - decomp;
			wg - web guard;
			kf - keyword filter;
			pbf - port-based framework;
			insp - content inspection;
			copt - content option;
			hopt - header option;
			dm - device map;
			ts - tcp stream;
			dev - device table;
			uf - url filter;
			cmd - command;
			rde - rule-based detection engine;
			ips - intrusion-prevention system;
			psd - port-scan-defense system;
			qos - smart qos;
			event - event;
			mpp - metadata protocol parser;
			re3 - resoft3 module;
			tld - top level domain filtering;
			dns - dns cache module;
			sb - dns redirect module;
			rdpage - redirect page;
			all - enable all components;
			all_pkt - trace all packets.
		Specify all necessary components to enable logging. Use space as a separator.
		Device Allocation: AP, SM"
	DEFVAL  { "all" }
	::= { dpi 4 }


dpiQoSAppRulesTable  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF DpiQoSAppRulesEntry
		MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS Application rules table
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		::= { dpi 15 }

dpiQoSAppRulesEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	DpiQoSAppRulesEntry
		MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS Application rules table entry
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		INDEX	{ dpiQoSAppRulesIndex }
		::= { dpiQoSAppRulesTable 1 }

DpiQoSAppRulesEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
		dpiQoSAppRulesIndex
				Integer32,
		dpiQoSAppID
				Integer32,
		dpiQoSAppPriority
				Integer32,
		dpiQoSAppRuleType
				Integer32
}

dpiQoSAppRulesIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..64)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS rules table limiting number,
			Table Entry is cleared if Index is set to zero.
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		::= { dpiQoSAppRulesEntry 1 }

dpiQoSAppID  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32 (0..65535)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS application id or qos group id,
			look dpiQosAppRuleType
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		::= { dpiQoSAppRulesEntry 2 }

dpiQoSAppPriority  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32(1..3)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS application piority, using as qos mark:
			1 - Voice
			2 - High
			3 - Low
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		::= { dpiQoSAppRulesEntry 3 }

dpiQoSAppRuleType  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX	   Integer32(0..1)
		MAX-ACCESS read-write
		STATUS	   current
		DESCRIPTION
			"dpi QoS application rule type:
			0 - qos application group rule,
			1 - single application rule
			Device Allocation: AP, STA"
		::= { dpiQoSAppRulesEntry 4 }
